-RRB-	O
.	O

:	O

-LSB-	O

-LRB-	O

Introduction	O
:	O
Calibration	O
transfer	O
-LRB-	O
CT	O
-RRB-	O
is	O
the	O
process	O
of	O
transferring	O
a	O
calibration	O
curve	O
from	O
one	O
instrument	O
to	O
another	O
or	O
from	O
one	O
set	O
of	O
environmental	O
conditions	O
to	O
another	O
without	O
the	O
need	O
to	O
resample	O
all	O
calibration	O
standards	O
.	O
This	O
task	O
is	O
especially	O
critical	O
in	O
space	O
science	O
where	O
extraterrestrial	O
instruments	O
calibrated	O
with	O
terrestrial	O
data	O
sets	O
are	O
used	O
.	O
For	O
example	O
,	O
the	O
current	O
calibration	O
target	O
set	O
for	O
the	O
ChemCam	O
LIBS	O
instrument	O
on	O
the	O
Curiosity	O
rover	O
-LSB-	O
1	O
-RSB-	O
includes	O
only	O
10	O
standards	O
,	O
so	O
Earth-based	O
laboratory	O
data	O
-LRB-	O
>	O
326	O
standards	O
-LSB-	O
2	O
-RSB-	O
-RRB-	O
are	O
being	O
used	O
to	O
develop	O
prediction	O
algorithms	O
for	O
Mars	O
data	O
that	O
assume	O
identical	O
instrument	O
performance	O
.	O
The	O
addition	O
of	O
CT	O
has	O
the	O
potential	O
to	O
improve	O
the	O
accuracy	O
of	O
Mars	O
predictions	O
by	O
aligning	O
laboratory	O
and	O
Mars	O
spectra	O
.	O
This	O
problem	O
is	O
not	O
unique	O
to	O
ChemCam	O
;	O
CT	O
can	O
be	O
used	O
to	O
augment	O
any	O
instrument	O
calibration	O
after	O
deployment	O
.	O
There	O
are	O
two	O
primary	O
ways	O
of	O
performing	O
CT	O
:	O
by	O
changing	O
the	O
weights	O
of	O
the	O
calibration	O
model	O
or	O
by	O
directly	O
modifying	O
lab-recorded	O
spectra	O
of	O
the	O
standards	O
to	O
align	O
them	O
with	O
those	O
on	O
Mars	O
.	O
This	O
research	O
uses	O
the	O
latter	O
method	O
,	O
where	O
CT	O
is	O
used	O
to	O
calculate	O
a	O
transformation	O
function	O
that	O
maps	O
spectra	O
from	O
one	O
condition	O
to	O
another	O
.	O
There	O
are	O
a	O
variety	O
of	O
methods	O
for	O
calculating	O
the	O
transfer	O
function	O
,	O
but	O
the	O
most	O
common	O
approach	O
relies	O
on	O
a	O
set	O
of	O
overlapping	O
standards	O
that	O
have	O
been	O
recorded	O
under	O
both	O
conditions	O
-LRB-	O
or	O
on	O
both	O
instruments	O
-RRB-	O
.	O
This	O
overlapping	O
subset	O
is	O
the	O
linking	O
set	O
between	O
the	O
two	O
data	O
sets	O
.	O
For	O
future	O
flight	O
instrument	O
design	O
,	O
it	O
is	O
important	O
to	O
know	O
the	O
minimum	O
size	O
of	O
an	O
effective	O
linking	O
set	O
.	O
So	O
here	O
we	O
examine	O
the	O
effectiveness	O
of	O
using	O
CT	O
while	O
varying	O
the	O
size	O
of	O
the	O
linking	O
set	O
.	O
To	O
answer	O
the	O
more	O
general	O
question	O
of	O
how	O
best	O
to	O
utilize	O
the	O
linking	O
set	O
,	O
three	O
meta-algorithms	O
that	O
do	O
not	O
use	O
CT	O
are	O
also	O
included	O
in	O
our	O
comparison	O
.	O
Lastly	O
,	O
we	O
explore	O
implementation	O
details	O
of	O
how	O
best	O
to	O
use	O
CT.	O
.	O

.	O

.	O

.	O

.	O
